English: 

pp1.2:1.1
Pali: <b>Dve puggalā—</b> 
English: 

pp1.2:2.1
Pali: Kodhano ca, upanāhī ca. 
English: 

pp1.2:3.1
Pali: Makkhī ca, paḷāsī ca. 
English: 

pp1.2:4.1
Pali: Issukī ca, maccharī ca. 
English: 

pp1.2:5.1
Pali: Saṭho ca, māyāvī ca. 
English: 

pp1.2:6.1
Pali: Ahiriko ca, anottappī ca. 
English: 

pp1.2:7.1
Pali: Dubbaco ca, pāpamitto ca. 
English: 

pp1.2:8.1
Pali: Indriyesu aguttadvāro ca, bhojane amattaññū ca. 
English: 

pp1.2:9.1
Pali: Muṭṭhassati ca, asampajāno ca. 
English: 

pp1.2:10.1
Pali: Sīlavipanno ca, diṭṭhivipanno ca. 
English: 

pp1.2:11.1
Pali: Ajjhattasaṁyojano ca, bahiddhāsaṁyojano ca. 
English: 

pp1.2:12.1
Pali: Akkodhano ca, anupanāhī ca. 
English: 

pp1.2:13.1
Pali: Amakkhī ca, apaḷāsī ca. 
English: 

pp1.2:14.1
Pali: Anissukī ca, amaccharī ca. 
English: 

pp1.2:15.1
Pali: Asaṭho ca, amāyāvī ca. 
English: 

pp1.2:16.1
Pali: Hirimā ca, ottappī ca. 
English: 

pp1.2:17.1
Pali: Suvaco ca, kalyāṇamitto ca. 
English: 

pp1.2:18.1
Pali: Indriyesu guttadvāro ca, bhojane mattaññū ca. 
English: 

pp1.2:19.1
Pali: Upaṭṭhitassati ca, sampajāno ca. 
English: 

pp1.2:20.1
Pali: Sīlasampanno ca, diṭṭhisampanno ca. 
English: 

pp1.2:21.1
Pali: Dve puggalā dullabhā lokasmiṁ. 
English: 

pp1.2:22.1
Pali: Dve puggalā duttappayā. 
English: 

pp1.2:23.1
Pali: Dve puggalā sutappayā. 
English: 

pp1.2:24.1
Pali: Dvinnaṁ puggalānaṁ āsavā vaḍḍhanti. 
English: 

pp1.2:25.1
Pali: Dvinnaṁ puggalānaṁ āsavā na vaḍḍhanti. 
English: 

pp1.2:26.1
Pali: Hīnādhimutto ca, paṇītādhimutto ca. 
English: 

pp1.2:27.1
Pali: Titto ca, tappetā ca. 
English: 

pp1.2:28.1
Pali: Dukaṁ.

pp1.3:0.3
Pali: 3. Tikauddesa 
English: 

pp1.3:1.1
Pali: <b>Tayo puggalā—</b> 
English: 

pp1.3:2.1
Pali: Nirāso, āsaṁso, vigatāso. 
English: 

pp1.3:3.1
Pali: Tayo gilānūpamā puggalā. 
English: 

pp1.3:4.1
Pali: Kāyasakkhī, diṭṭhippatto, saddhāvimutto. 
English: 

pp1.3:5.1
Pali: Gūthabhāṇī, pupphabhāṇī, madhubhāṇī. 
English: 

pp1.3:6.1
Pali: Arukūpamacitto puggalo, vijjūpamacitto puggalo, vajirūpamacitto puggalo. 
English: 

pp1.3:7.1
Pali: Andho, ekacakkhu, dvicakkhu. 
English: 

pp1.3:8.1
Pali: Avakujjapañño puggalo, ucchaṅgapañño puggalo, puthupañño puggalo. 
English: 

pp1.3:9.1
Pali: Atthekacco puggalo kāmesu ca bhavesu ca avītarāgo, atthekacco puggalo kāmesu vītarāgo bhavesu avītarāgo, atthekacco puggalo kāmesu ca bhavesu ca vītarāgo. 
English: 

pp1.3:10.1
Pali: Pāsāṇalekhūpamo puggalo, pathavilekhūpamo puggalo, udakalekhūpamo puggalo. 
English: 

pp1.3:11.1
Pali: Tayo potthakūpamā puggalā. 
English: 

pp1.3:12.1
Pali: Tayo kāsikavatthūpamā puggalā. 
English: 

pp1.3:13.1
Pali: Suppameyyo, duppameyyo, appameyyo. 
English: 

pp1.3:14.1
Pali: Atthekacco puggalo na sevitabbo na bhajitabbo na payirupāsitabbo, atthekacco puggalo sevitabbo bhajitabbo payirupāsitabbo, atthekacco puggalo sakkatvā garuṁ katvā sevitabbo bhajitabbo payirupāsitabbo. 
English: 

pp1.3:15.1
Pali: Atthekacco puggalo jigucchitabbo na sevitabbo na bhajitabbo na payirupāsitabbo, atthekacco puggalo ajjhupekkhitabbo na sevitabbo na bhajitabbo na payirupāsitabbo; 
English: 

pp1.3:15.2
Pali: atthekacco puggalo sevitabbo bhajitabbo payirupāsitabbo. 
English: 

pp1.3:16.1
Pali: Atthekacco puggalo sīlesu paripūrakārī, samādhismiṁ mattaso kārī, paññāya mattaso kārī; 
English: 

pp1.3:16.2
Pali: atthekacco puggalo sīlesu ca paripūrakārī, samādhismiñca paripūrakārī, paññāya mattaso kārī; 
English: 

pp1.3:16.3
Pali: atthekacco puggalo sīlesu ca paripūrakārī, samādhismiñca paripūrakārī, paññāya ca paripūrakārī. 
English: 

pp1.3:17.1
Pali: Tayo satthāro. 
English: 

pp1.3:18.1
Pali: Aparepi tayo satthāro. 
English: 

pp1.3:19.1
Pali: Tikaṁ. 
English:

pp1.4:16.1
Pali: Atthekacco puggalo ananuvicca apariyogāhetvā avaṇṇārahassa vaṇṇaṁ bhāsitā hoti, atthekacco puggalo ananuvicca apariyogāhetvā vaṇṇārahassa avaṇṇaṁ bhāsitā hoti, atthekacco puggalo ananuvicca apariyogāhetvā appasādanīye ṭhāne pasādaṁ upadaṁsitā hoti, atthekacco puggalo ananuvicca apariyogāhetvā pasādanīye ṭhāne appasādaṁ upadaṁsitā hoti.

English: 

pp1.4:18.1
Pali: Atthekacco puggalo avaṇṇārahassa avaṇṇaṁ bhāsitā hoti bhūtaṁ tacchaṁ kālena, no ca kho vaṇṇārahassa vaṇṇaṁ bhāsitā hoti bhūtaṁ tacchaṁ kālena; 
English: 

pp1.4:18.2
Pali: atthekacco puggalo vaṇṇārahassa vaṇṇaṁ bhāsitā hoti bhūtaṁ tacchaṁ kālena, no ca kho avaṇṇārahassa avaṇṇaṁ bhāsitā hoti bhūtaṁ tacchaṁ kālena; 
English: 

pp1.4:18.3
Pali: atthekacco puggalo avaṇṇārahassa ca avaṇṇaṁ bhāsitā hoti bhūtaṁ tacchaṁ kālena; 
English: 

pp1.4:18.4
Pali: vaṇṇārahassa ca vaṇṇaṁ bhāsitā hoti bhūtaṁ tacchaṁ kālena, atthekacco puggalo neva avaṇṇārahassa avaṇṇaṁ bhāsitā hoti bhūtaṁ tacchaṁ kālena, no ca vaṇṇārahassa vaṇṇaṁ bhāsitā hoti bhūtaṁ tacchaṁ kālena. 
English: 

pp1.4:19.1
Pali: Uṭṭhānaphalūpajīvī no puññaphalūpajīvī, puññaphalūpajīvī no uṭṭhānaphalūpajīvī, uṭṭhānaphalūpajīvī ca puññaphalūpajīvī ca, neva uṭṭhānaphalūpajīvī no puññaphalūpajīvī. 
English: 

pp1.4:20.1
Pali: Tamo tamaparāyano, tamo jotiparāyano, joti tamaparāyano, joti jotiparāyano. 
English: 

pp1.4:21.1
Pali: Oṇatoṇato, oṇatuṇṇato, uṇṇatoṇato, uṇṇatuṇṇato. 
English: 

pp1.4:22.1
Pali: Cattāro rukkhūpamā puggalā.

pp1.4:23.1

pp1.4:25.1

English: 

pp1.4:25.4
Pali: atthekacco puggalo neva attahitāya paṭipanno hoti no parahitāya. 
English: 

pp1.4:26.1
Pali: Atthekacco puggalo attantapo hoti attaparitāpanānuyogamanuyutto; 
English: 

pp1.4:26.2
Pali: atthekacco puggalo parantapo hoti paraparitāpanānuyogamanuyutto; 
English: 

pp1.4:26.3
Pali: atthekacco puggalo attantapo ca hoti attaparitāpanānuyogamanuyutto, parantapo ca paraparitāpanānuyogamanuyutto; 
English: 

pp1.4:26.4
Pali: atthekacco puggalo neva attantapo hoti na attaparitāpanānuyogamanuyutto, na parantapo na paraparitāpanānuyogamanuyutto. 
English: 

pp1.4:26.5
Pali: So anattantapo aparantapo diṭṭheva dhamme nicchāto nibbuto sītībhūto sukhappaṭisaṁvedī brahmabhūtena attanā viharati. 
English: 

pp1.4:27.1
Pali: Sarāgo, sadoso, samoho, samāno. 
English: 

pp1.4:28.1
Pali: Atthekacco puggalo lābhī hoti ajjhattaṁ cetosamathassa, na lābhī adhipaññādhammavipassanāya; 
English: 

pp1.4:28.2
Pali: atthekacco puggalo lābhī hoti adhipaññādhammavipassanāya, na lābhī ajjhattaṁ cetosamathassa; 
English: 

pp1.4:28.3
Pali: atthekacco puggalo lābhī ceva hoti ajjhattaṁ cetosamathassa, lābhī ca adhipaññādhammavipassanāya; 
English: 

pp1.4:28.4
Pali: atthekacco puggalo neva lābhī hoti ajjhattaṁ cetosamathassa, na lābhī adhipaññādhammavipassanāya. 
English: 

pp1.4:29.1
Pali: Anusotagāmī puggalo, paṭisotagāmī puggalo, ṭhitatto puggalo, tiṇṇo pāraṅgato thale tiṭṭhati brāhmaṇo. 
English:

English:

English: 

pp1.5:2.1
Pali: Atthekacco puggalo ārabhati ca vippaṭisārī ca hoti, tañca cetovimuttiṁ paññāvimuttiṁ yathābhūtaṁ nappajānāti, yatthassa te uppannā pāpakā akusalā dhammā aparisesā nirujjhanti. 
English: 

pp1.5:2.2
Pali: Atthekacco puggalo ārabhati na vippaṭisārī ca hoti, tañca cetovimuttiṁ paññāvimuttiṁ yathābhūtaṁ nappajānāti, yatthassa te uppannā pāpakā akusalā dhammā aparisesā nirujjhanti. 
English: 

pp1.5:2.3
Pali: Atthekacco puggalo nārabhati vippaṭisārī ca hoti, tañca cetovimuttiṁ paññāvimuttiṁ yathābhūtaṁ nappajānāti, yatthassa te uppannā pāpakā akusalā dhammā aparisesā nirujjhanti. 
English: 

pp1.5:2.4
Pali: Atthekacco puggalo nārabhati na vippaṭisārī hoti, tañca cetovimuttiṁ paññāvimuttiṁ yathābhūtaṁ nappajānāti, yatthassa te uppannā pāpakā akusalā dhammā aparisesā nirujjhanti. 
English: 

pp1.5:2.5
Pali: Atthekacco puggalo nārabhati na vippaṭisārī hoti, tañca cetovimuttiṁ paññāvimuttiṁ yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, yatthassa te uppannā pāpakā akusalā dhammā aparisesā nirujjhanti. 
English:

pp1.6:0.3
Pali: 6. Chakkauddesa 
English: 

pp1.6:1.1
Pali: <b>Cha puggalā—</b> 
English: 

pp1.6:2.1
Pali: Atthekacco puggalo pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu sāmaṁ saccāni abhisambujjhati, tattha ca sabbaññutaṁ pāpuṇāti balesu ca vasībhāvaṁ. 
English: 

pp1.6:2.2
Pali: Atthekacco puggalo pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu sāmaṁ saccāni abhisambujjhati, na ca tattha sabbaññutaṁ pāpuṇāti na ca balesu vasībhāvaṁ. 
English: 

pp1.6:2.3
Pali: Atthekacco puggalo pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu sāmaṁ saccāni anabhisambujjhati, diṭṭhe ceva dhamme dukkhassantakaro hoti sāvakapāramiñca pāpuṇāti. 
English: 

pp1.6:2.4
Pali: Atthekacco puggalo pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu sāmaṁ saccāni anabhisambujjhati, diṭṭheva dhamme dukkhassantakaro hoti, na ca sāvakapāramiṁ pāpuṇāti. 
English: 

pp1.6:2.5
Pali: Atthekacco puggalo pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu sāmaṁ saccāni anabhisambujjhati, na ca diṭṭheva dhamme dukkhassantakaro hoti, anāgāmī hoti anāgantā itthattaṁ. 
English: 

pp1.6:2.6
Pali: Atthekacco puggalo pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu sāmaṁ saccāni anabhisambujjhati, na ca diṭṭheva dhamme dukkhassantakaro hoti, āgāmī hoti āgantā itthattaṁ. 
English: 

pp1.6:3.1
Pali: Chakkaṁ. 
English:

Pali: 1. Ekakapuggalapaññatti 
English: 

pp2.1:1.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo samayavimutto? 
English: 

pp2.1:1.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo kālena kālaṁ samayena samayaṁ aṭṭha vimokkhe kāyena phusitvā viharati, paññāya cassa disvā ekacce āsavā parikkhīṇā honti—
English: 

pp2.1:1.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati puggalo “samayavimutto”. 
English: 

pp2.1:2.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo asamayavimutto? 
English: 

pp2.1:2.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo na heva kho kālena kālaṁ samayena samayaṁ aṭṭha vimokkhe kāyena phusitvā viharati, paññāya cassa disvā āsavā parikkhīṇā honti—
English: 

pp2.1:2.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati puggalo “asamayavimutto”. 
English: 

pp2.1:2.4
Pali: Sabbepi ariyapuggalā ariye vimokkhe asamayavimuttā. 
English: 

pp2.1:3.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo kuppadhammo? 
English: 

pp2.1:3.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo lābhī hoti rūpasahagatānaṁ vā arūpasahagatānaṁ vā samāpattīnaṁ. 
English: 

pp2.1:3.3
Pali: So ca kho na nikāmalābhī hoti na akicchalābhī na akasiralābhī; 
English: 

pp2.1:3.4
Pali: na yatthicchakaṁ yadicchakaṁ yāvaticchakaṁ samāpajjatipi vuṭṭhātipi. 
English: 

pp2.1:3.5
Pali: Ṭhānaṁ kho panetaṁ vijjati, yaṁ tassa puggalassa pamādamāgamma tā samāpattiyo kuppeyyuṁ—
English: 

pp2.1:3.6
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati puggalo “kuppadhammo”. 
English: 

pp2.1:4.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo akuppadhammo? 
English: 

pp2.1:4.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo lābhī hoti rūpasahagatānaṁ vā arūpasahagatānaṁ vā samāpattīnaṁ.

Pali: So ca kho nikāmalābhī hoti akicchalābhī akasiralābhī; 
English: 

pp2.1:4.4

English:

English:

Pali: ayaṁ vuccati puggalo “akuppadhammo”. 
English:

pp2.1:5.1

pp2.1:7.1

pp2.1:9.1

pp2.1:9.4

pp2.1:10.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo gotrabhū?

pp2.1:12.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo abhabbāgamano? 
English:

English: 

pp2.1:12.3
Pali: ime vuccanti puggalā “abhabbāgamanā”. 
English: 

pp2.1:13.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo bhabbāgamano? 
English: 

pp2.1:13.2
Pali: Ye te puggalā na kammāvaraṇena samannāgatā, na kilesāvaraṇena samannāgatā, na vipākāvaraṇena samannāgatā, saddhā chandikā paññavanto aneḷā, bhabbā niyāmaṁ okkamituṁ kusalesu dhammesu sammattaṁ—
English: 

pp2.1:13.3
Pali: ime vuccanti puggalā “bhabbāgamanā”.

English: 

pp2.1:14.2

English: 

pp2.1:14.3

English:

English:

Pali: Katamo ca puggalo samasīsī? 
English:

Pali: paññāya cassa disvā āsavā parikkhīṇā honti.

English: 

pp2.1:27.3
Pali: Tathāgatappaveditā cassa dhammā paññāya vodiṭṭhā honti vocaritā.

pp2.1:27.5

English: 

pp2.1:28.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo saddhāvimutto? 
English: 

pp2.1:28.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo “idaṁ dukkhan”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, “ayaṁ dukkhasamudayo”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, “ayaṁ dukkhanirodho”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, “ayaṁ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti. 
English: 

pp2.1:28.3
Pali: Tathāgatappaveditā cassa dhammā paññāya vodiṭṭhā honti vocaritā.

English: 

pp2.1:40.3
Pali: So avihā cuto atappaṁ gacchati, atappā cuto sudassaṁ gacchati, sudassā cuto sudassiṁ gacchati, sudassiyā cuto akaniṭṭhaṁ gacchati;

Pali: 2. Dukapuggalapaññatti 
English: 

pp2.2:1.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo kodhano? 
English: 

pp2.2:1.2
Pali: Tattha katamo kodho? 
English: 

pp2.2:1.3
Pali: Yo kodho kujjhanā kujjhitattaṁ doso dussanā dussitattaṁ byāpatti byāpajjanā byāpajjitattaṁ virodho paṭivirodho caṇḍikkaṁ asuropo anattamanatā cittassa—
English: 

pp2.2:1.4
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati kodho. 
English: 

pp2.2:1.5
Pali: Yassa puggalassa ayaṁ kodho appahīno—
English: 

pp2.2:1.6
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati puggalo “kodhano”. 
English: 

pp2.2:2.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo upanāhī? 
English: 

pp2.2:2.2
Pali: Tattha katamo upanāho? 
English: 

pp2.2:2.3
Pali: Pubbakālaṁ kodho aparakālaṁ upanāho. 
English: 

pp2.2:2.4
Pali: Yo evarūpo upanāho upanayhanā upanayhitattaṁ aṭṭhapanā ṭhapanā saṇṭhapanā anusaṁsandanā anuppabandhanā daḷhīkammaṁ kodhassa—
English: 

pp2.2:2.5
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati upanāho. 
English: 

pp2.2:2.6
Pali: Yassa puggalassa ayaṁ upanāho appahīno—
English: 

pp2.2:2.7
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati puggalo “upanāhī”.

English: 

pp2.2:8.4

English: 

pp2.2:8.5
Pali: Yā evarūpā māyā māyāvitā accāsarā vañcanā nikati vikiraṇā pariharaṇā gūhanā parigūhanā chādanā paṭicchādanā anuttānīkammaṁ anāvikammaṁ vocchādanā pāpakiriyā—

Pali: imesaṁ dvinnaṁ puggalānaṁ āsavā vaḍḍhanti. 
English: 

pp2.2:43.1
Pali: Katamesaṁ dvinnaṁ puggalānaṁ āsavā na vaḍḍhanti? 
English: 

pp2.2:43.2
Pali: Yo ca na kukkuccāyitabbaṁ na kukkuccāyati, yo ca kukkuccāyitabbaṁ kukkuccāyati—
English: 

pp2.2:43.3
Pali: imesaṁ dvinnaṁ puggalānaṁ āsavā na vaḍḍhanti. 
English: 

pp2.2:44.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo hīnādhimutto? 
English: 

pp2.2:44.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo dussīlo hoti pāpadhammo, so aññaṁ dussīlaṁ pāpadhammaṁ sevati bhajati payirupāsati—
English: 

pp2.2:44.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati puggalo “hīnādhimutto”. 
English: 

pp2.2:45.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo paṇītādhimutto? 
English: 

pp2.2:45.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo sīlavā hoti kalyāṇadhammo, so aññaṁ sīlavantaṁ kalyāṇadhammaṁ sevati bhajati payirupāsati—
English: 

pp2.2:45.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati puggalo “paṇītādhimutto”. 
English: 

pp2.2:46.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo titto? 
English: 

pp2.2:46.2
Pali: Paccekasambuddhā ye ca tathāgatassa sāvakā arahanto tittā. 
English: 

pp2.2:46.3
Pali: Sammāsambuddho titto ca tappetā ca. 
English:

Pali: Dukaniddeso.

pp2.3:0.3
Pali: 3. Tikapuggalapaññatti 
English: 

pp2.3:1.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo nirāso? 
English: 

pp2.3:1.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo dussīlo hoti pāpadhammo asuci saṅkassarasamācāro paṭicchannakammanto assamaṇo samaṇapaṭiñño abrahmacārī brahmacāripaṭiñño antopūti avassuto kasambujāto. 
English: 

pp2.3:1.3
Pali: So suṇāti—
English: 

pp2.3:1.4
Pali: “itthannāmo kira bhikkhu āsavānaṁ khayā anāsavaṁ cetovimuttiṁ paññāvimuttiṁ diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṁ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharatī”ti. 
English: 

pp2.3:1.5
Pali: Tassa na evaṁ hoti—
English: 

pp2.3:1.6
Pali: “kudāssu nāmāhampi āsavānaṁ khayā anāsavaṁ cetovimuttiṁ paññāvimuttiṁ diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṁ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharissāmī”ti. 
English: 

pp2.3:1.7
Pali: Ayaṁ vuccati puggalo “nirāso”. 
English: 

pp2.3:2.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo āsaṁso? 
English: 

pp2.3:2.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo sīlavā hoti kalyāṇadhammo. 
English: 

pp2.3:2.3
Pali: So suṇāti—
English: 

pp2.3:2.4
Pali: “itthannāmo kira bhikkhu āsavānaṁ khayā anāsavaṁ cetovimuttiṁ paññāvimuttiṁ diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṁ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharatī”ti. 
English: 

pp2.3:2.5
Pali: Tassa evaṁ hoti—
English: 

pp2.3:2.6
Pali: “kudāssu nāmāhampi āsavānaṁ khayā anāsavaṁ cetovimuttiṁ paññāvimuttiṁ diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṁ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharissāmī”ti. 
English: 

pp2.3:2.7
Pali: Ayaṁ vuccati puggalo “āsaṁso”.

pp2.3:3.1

English: 

pp2.3:3.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo āsavānaṁ khayā anāsavaṁ cetovimuttiṁ paññāvimuttiṁ diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṁ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharati.

Pali: So suṇāti—

pp2.3:3.7
Pali: Taṁ kissa hetu?

Pali: Ayaṁ vuccati puggalo “vigatāso”. 
English: 

pp2.3:4.1
Pali: Tattha katame tayo gilānūpamā puggalā? 
English: 

pp2.3:4.2
Pali: Tayo gilānā—
English: 

pp2.3:4.3
Pali: idhekacco gilāno labhanto vā sappāyāni bhojanāni alabhanto vā sappāyāni bhojanāni, labhanto vā sappāyāni bhesajjāni alabhanto vā sappāyāni bhesajjāni, labhanto vā patirūpaṁ upaṭṭhākaṁ alabhanto vā patirūpaṁ upaṭṭhākaṁ, neva vuṭṭhāti tamhā ābādhā. 
English: 

pp2.3:5.1
Pali: Idha panekacco gilāno labhanto vā sappāyāni bhojanāni alabhanto vā sappāyāni bhojanāni, labhanto vā sappāyāni bhesajjāni alabhanto vā sappāyāni bhesajjāni, labhanto vā patirūpaṁ upaṭṭhākaṁ alabhanto vā patirūpaṁ upaṭṭhākaṁ, vuṭṭhāti tamhā ābādhā. 
English: 

pp2.3:6.1
Pali: Idha panekacco gilāno labhanto sappāyāni bhojanāni no alabhanto, labhanto sappāyāni bhesajjāni no alabhanto, labhanto patirūpaṁ upaṭṭhākaṁ no alabhanto, vuṭṭhāti tamhā ābādhā. 
English: 

pp2.3:7.1
Pali: Tatra yvāyaṁ gilāno labhanto sappāyāni bhojanāni no alabhanto, labhanto sappāyāni bhesajjāni no alabhanto, labhanto patirūpaṁ upaṭṭhākaṁ no alabhanto, vuṭṭhāti tamhā ābādhā, imaṁ gilānaṁ paṭicca bhagavatā gilānabhattaṁ anuññātaṁ gilānabhesajjaṁ anuññātaṁ gilānupaṭṭhāko anuññāto. 
English: 

pp2.3:7.2
Pali: Imañca pana gilānaṁ paṭicca aññepi gilānā upaṭṭhātabbā. 
English: 

pp2.3:8.1
Pali: Evamevaṁ tayo gilānūpamā puggalā santo saṁvijjamānā lokasmiṁ. 
English: 

pp2.3:8.2
Pali: Katame tayo? 
English: 

pp2.3:8.3
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo labhanto vā tathāgataṁ dassanāya alabhanto vā tathāgataṁ dassanāya, labhanto vā tathāgatappaveditaṁ dhammavinayaṁ savaṇāya alabhanto vā tathāgatappaveditaṁ dhammavinayaṁ savaṇāya, neva okkamati niyāmaṁ kusalesu dhammesu sammattaṁ. 
English: 

pp2.3:9.1
Pali: Idha panekacco puggalo labhanto vā tathāgataṁ dassanāya alabhanto vā tathāgataṁ dassanāya, labhanto vā tathāgatappaveditaṁ dhammavinayaṁ savaṇāya alabhanto vā tathāgatappaveditaṁ dhammavinayaṁ savaṇāya, okkamati niyāmaṁ kusalesu dhammesu sammattaṁ. 
English: 

pp2.3:10.1
Pali: Idha panekacco puggalo labhanto tathāgataṁ dassanāya no alabhanto, labhanto tathāgatappaveditaṁ dhammavinayaṁ savaṇāya no alabhanto, okkamati niyāmaṁ kusalesu dhammesu sammattaṁ. 
English: 

pp2.3:11.1
Pali: Tatra yvāyaṁ puggalo labhanto tathāgataṁ dassanāya no alabhanto, labhanto tathāgatappaveditaṁ dhammavinayaṁ savaṇāya no alabhanto, okkamati niyāmaṁ kusalesu dhammesu sammattaṁ, imaṁ puggalaṁ paṭicca bhagavatā dhammadesanā anuññātā, imañca puggalaṁ paṭicca aññesampi dhammo desetabbo. 
English: 

pp2.3:11.2
Pali: Ime tayo gilānūpamā puggalā santo saṁvijjamānā lokasmiṁ.

pp2.3:12.1

English: 

pp2.3:12.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo aṭṭha vimokkhe kāyena phusitvā viharati, paññāya cassa disvā ekacce āsavā parikkhīṇā honti—
English: 

pp2.3:12.3

pp2.3:13.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo diṭṭhippatto? 
English: 

pp2.3:13.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo “idaṁ dukkhan”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, “ayaṁ dukkhasamudayo”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, “ayaṁ dukkhanirodho”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, “ayaṁ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, tathāgatappaveditā cassa dhammā paññāya vodiṭṭhā honti vocaritā, paññāya cassa disvā ekacce āsavā parikkhīṇā honti—

pp2.3:21.3

pp2.3:22.3

pp2.3:24.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo avakujjapañño? 
English: 

pp2.3:24.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo ārāmaṁ gantā hoti abhikkhaṇaṁ bhikkhūnaṁ santike dhammassavaṇāya. 
English: 

pp2.3:24.3
Pali: Tassa bhikkhū dhammaṁ desenti ādikalyāṇaṁ majjhekalyāṇaṁ pariyosānakalyāṇaṁ sātthaṁ sabyañjanaṁ kevalaparipuṇṇaṁ parisuddhaṁ brahmacariyaṁ pakāsenti. 
English: 

pp2.3:24.4
Pali: So tasmiṁ āsane nisinno tassā kathāya neva ādiṁ manasi karoti, na majjhaṁ manasi karoti, na pariyosānaṁ manasi karoti. 
English: 

pp2.3:24.5
Pali: Vuṭṭhitopi tamhā āsanā tassā kathāya neva ādiṁ manasi karoti, na majjhaṁ manasi karoti, na pariyosānaṁ manasi karoti. 
English: 

pp2.3:24.6
Pali: Seyyathāpi nāma kumbho nikkujjo tatra udakaṁ āsittaṁ vivaṭṭati, no saṇṭhāti; 
English: 

pp2.3:24.7
Pali: evamevaṁ idhekacco puggalo ārāmaṁ gantā hoti abhikkhaṇaṁ bhikkhūnaṁ santike dhammassavaṇāya. 
English: 

pp2.3:24.8
Pali: Tassa bhikkhū dhammaṁ desenti ādikalyāṇaṁ majjhekalyāṇaṁ pariyosānakalyāṇaṁ sātthaṁ sabyañjanaṁ kevalaparipuṇṇaṁ parisuddhaṁ brahmacariyaṁ pakāsenti. 
English: 

pp2.3:24.9

English: 

pp2.3:24.10
Pali: Vuṭṭhitopi tamhā āsanā tassā kathāya neva ādiṁ manasi karoti, na majjhaṁ manasi karoti, na pariyosānaṁ manasi karoti—

pp2.3:25.1

English: 

pp2.3:25.2

pp2.3:25.3
Pali: Tassa bhikkhū dhammaṁ desenti ādikalyāṇaṁ majjhekalyāṇaṁ pariyosānakalyāṇaṁ sātthaṁ sabyañjanaṁ kevalaparipuṇṇaṁ parisuddhaṁ brahmacariyaṁ pakāsenti.

pp2.3:25.4

English: 

pp2.3:47.4
Pali: Seyyathāpi nāma tindukālātaṁ kaṭṭhena vā kaṭhalāya vā ghaṭṭitaṁ bhiyyoso mattāya cicciṭāyati ciṭiciṭāyati; 
English: 

pp2.3:47.5
Pali: evamevaṁ idhekacco puggalo kodhano hoti upāyāsabahulo, appampi vutto samāno abhisajjati kuppati byāpajjati patitthīyati, kopañca dosañca appaccayañca pātukaroti. 
English: 

pp2.3:47.6
Pali: Seyyathāpi nāma gūthakūpo kaṭṭhena vā kaṭhalāya vā ghaṭṭito bhiyyoso mattāya duggandho hoti; 
English: 

pp2.3:47.7
Pali: evamevaṁ idhekacco puggalo kodhano hoti upāyāsabahulo, appampi vutto samāno abhisajjati kuppati byāpajjati patitthīyati, kopañca dosañca appaccayañca pātukaroti; 
English: 

pp2.3:47.8
Pali: evarūpo puggalo ajjhupekkhitabbo na sevitabbo na bhajitabbo na payirupāsitabbo. 
English: 

pp2.3:47.9
Pali: Taṁ kissa hetu? 
English: 

pp2.3:47.10
Pali: “Akkoseyyapi maṁ paribhāseyyapi maṁ anatthampi me kareyyā”ti. 
English: 

pp2.3:47.11
Pali: Tasmā evarūpo puggalo ajjhupekkhitabbo na sevitabbo na bhajitabbo na payirupāsitabbo. 
English: 

pp2.3:48.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo sevitabbo bhajitabbo payirupāsitabbo? 
English: 

pp2.3:48.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo sīlavā hoti kalyāṇadhammo—
English: 

pp2.3:48.3
Pali: evarūpo puggalo sevitabbo bhajitabbo payirupāsitabbo. 
English: 

pp2.3:48.4
Pali: Taṁ kissa hetu? 
English: 

pp2.3:48.5
Pali: Kiñcāpi evarūpassa puggalassa na diṭṭhānugatiṁ āpajjati, atha kho naṁ kalyāṇo kittisaddo abbhuggacchati—
English: 

pp2.3:48.6
Pali: “kalyāṇamitto purisapuggalo kalyāṇasahāyo kalyāṇasampavaṅko”ti. 
English: 

pp2.3:48.7
Pali: Tasmā evarūpo puggalo sevitabbo bhajitabbo payirupāsitabbo. 
English: 

pp2.3:49.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo sīlesu paripūrakārī, samādhismiṁ mattaso kārī, paññāya mattaso kārī? 
English: 

pp2.3:49.2
Pali: Sotāpannasakadāgāmino—
English: 

pp2.3:49.3
Pali: ime vuccanti puggalā sīlesu paripūrakārino, samādhismiṁ mattaso kārino, paññāya mattaso kārino. 
English: 

pp2.3:50.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo sīlesu ca paripūrakārī, samādhismiñca paripūrakārī, paññāya mattaso kārī? 
English: 

pp2.3:50.2
Pali: Anāgāmī—
English: 

pp2.3:50.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati puggalo sīlesu ca paripūrakārī, samādhismiñca paripūrakārī, paññāya mattaso kārī. 
English: 

pp2.3:51.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo sīlesu ca paripūrakārī, samādhismiñca paripūrakārī, paññāya ca paripūrakārī? 
English: 

pp2.3:51.2
Pali: Arahā—
English: 

pp2.3:51.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati puggalo sīlesu ca paripūrakārī, samādhismiñca paripūrakārī, paññāya ca paripūrakārī. 
English: 

pp2.3:52.1
Pali: Tattha katame tayo satthāro? 
English: 

pp2.3:52.2
Pali: Idhekacco satthā kāmānaṁ pariññaṁ paññapeti, na rūpānaṁ pariññaṁ paññapeti, na vedanānaṁ pariññaṁ paññapeti. 
English: 

pp2.3:52.3
Pali: Idha panekacco satthā kāmānañca pariññaṁ paññapeti, rūpānañca pariññaṁ paññapeti, na vedanānaṁ pariññaṁ paññapeti. 
English: 

pp2.3:52.4
Pali: Idha panekacco satthā kāmānañca pariññaṁ paññapeti, rūpānañca pariññaṁ paññapeti, vedanānañca pariññaṁ paññapeti. 
English: 

pp2.3:53.1
Pali: Tatra yvāyaṁ satthā kāmānaṁ pariññaṁ paññapeti, na rūpānaṁ pariññaṁ paññapeti, na vedanānaṁ pariññaṁ paññapeti, rūpāvacarasamāpattiyā lābhī satthā tena daṭṭhabbo. 
English: 

pp2.3:53.2
Pali: Tatra yvāyaṁ satthā kāmānañca pariññaṁ paññapeti, rūpānañca pariññaṁ paññapeti, na vedanānaṁ pariññaṁ paññapeti, arūpāvacarasamāpattiyā lābhī satthā tena daṭṭhabbo. 
English: 

pp2.3:53.3
Pali: Tatra yvāyaṁ satthā kāmānañca pariññaṁ paññapeti, rūpānañca pariññaṁ paññapeti, vedanānañca pariññaṁ paññapeti, sammāsambuddho satthā tena daṭṭhabbo. 
English: 

pp2.3:53.4
Pali: Ime tayo satthāro. 
English: 

pp2.3:54.1
Pali: Tattha katame aparepi tayo satthāro? 
English: 

pp2.3:54.2
Pali: Idhekacco satthā diṭṭhe ceva dhamme attānaṁ saccato thetato paññapeti, abhisamparāyañca attānaṁ saccato thetato paññapeti. 
English: 

pp2.3:54.3
Pali: Idha panekacco satthā diṭṭhe ceva dhamme attānaṁ saccato thetato paññapeti, no ca kho abhisamparāyaṁ attānaṁ saccato thetato paññapeti. 
English: 

pp2.3:54.4
Pali: Idha panekacco satthā diṭṭhe ceva dhamme attānaṁ saccato thetato na paññapeti, abhisamparāyañca attānaṁ saccato thetato na paññapeti. 
English: 

pp2.3:55.1
Pali: Tatra yvāyaṁ satthā diṭṭhe ceva dhamme attānaṁ saccato thetato paññapeti, abhisamparāyañca attānaṁ saccato thetato paññapeti, sassatavādo satthā tena daṭṭhabbo. 
English: 

pp2.3:55.2
Pali: Tatra yvāyaṁ satthā diṭṭhe ceva dhamme attānaṁ saccato thetato paññapeti, no ca kho abhisamparāyaṁ attānaṁ saccato thetato paññapeti, ucchedavādo satthā tena daṭṭhabbo. 
English: 

pp2.3:55.3
Pali: Tatra yvāyaṁ satthā diṭṭhe ceva dhamme attānaṁ saccato thetato na paññapeti, abhisamparāyañca attānaṁ saccato thetato na paññapeti, sammāsambuddho satthā tena daṭṭhabbo. 
English: 

pp2.3:55.4
Pali: Ime aparepi tayo satthāro. 
English: 

pp2.3:56.1
Pali: Tikaniddeso. 
English:

pp2.4:0.3
Pali: 4. Catukkapuggalapaññatti 
English: 

pp2.4:1.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo asappuriso? 
English: 

pp2.4:1.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo pāṇātipātī hoti, adinnādāyī hoti, kāmesumicchācārī hoti, musāvādī hoti, surāmerayamajjapamādaṭṭhāyī hoti—
English: 

pp2.4:1.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati puggalo “asappuriso”. 
English: 

pp2.4:2.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo asappurisena asappurisataro? 
English: 

pp2.4:2.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo attanā ca pāṇātipātī hoti parañca pāṇātipāte samādapeti, attanā ca adinnādāyī hoti parañca adinnādāne samādapeti, attanā ca kāmesumicchācārī hoti parañca kāmesumicchācāre samādapeti, attanā ca musāvādī hoti parañca musāvāde samādapeti, attanā ca surāmerayamajjapamādaṭṭhāyī hoti parañca surāmerayamajjapamādaṭṭhāne samādapeti—
English: 

pp2.4:2.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati puggalo “asappurisena asappurisataro”. 
English: 

pp2.4:3.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo sappuriso? 
English: 

pp2.4:3.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo pāṇātipātā paṭivirato hoti, adinnādānā paṭivirato hoti, kāmesumicchācārā paṭivirato hoti, musāvādā paṭivirato hoti, surāmerayamajjapamādaṭṭhānā paṭivirato hoti—
English: 

pp2.4:3.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati puggalo “sappuriso”. 
English:

Pali: Katamo ca puggalo sappurisena sappurisataro? 
English: 

pp2.4:4.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo attanā ca pāṇātipātā paṭivirato hoti parañca pāṇātipātā veramaṇiyā samādapeti, attanā ca adinnādānā paṭivirato hoti parañca adinnādānā veramaṇiyā samādapeti, attanā ca kāmesumicchācārā paṭivirato hoti parañca kāmesumicchācārā veramaṇiyā samādapeti, attanā ca musāvādā paṭivirato hoti parañca musāvādā veramaṇiyā samādapeti, attanā ca surāmerayamajjapamādaṭṭhānā paṭivirato hoti parañca surāmerayamajjapamādaṭṭhānā veramaṇiyā samādapeti—

pp2.4:110.1
Pali: Kathañca puggalo attantapo hoti attaparitāpanānuyogamanuyutto? 
English: 

pp2.4:110.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo acelako hoti muttācāro hatthāpalekhano, naehibhaddantiko natiṭṭhabhaddantiko nābhihaṭaṁ na uddissakataṁ na nimantanaṁ sādiyati, so na kumbhimukhā paṭiggaṇhāti na kaḷopimukhā paṭiggaṇhāti, na eḷakamantaraṁ na daṇḍamantaraṁ na musalamantaraṁ na dvinnaṁ bhuñjamānānaṁ na gabbhiniyā na pāyamānāya na purisantaragatāya, na saṅkittīsu na yattha sā upaṭṭhito hoti na yattha makkhikā saṇḍasaṇḍacārinī, na macchaṁ na maṁsaṁ na suraṁ na merayaṁ na thusodakaṁ pivati. 
English: 

pp2.4:110.3
Pali: So ekāgāriko vā hoti ekālopiko, dvāgāriko vā hoti dvālopiko …pe… 
English: 

pp2.4:110.4
Pali: sattāgāriko vā hoti sattālopiko; 
English: 

pp2.4:110.5
Pali: ekissāpi dattiyā yāpeti, dvīhipi dattīhi yāpeti …pe… 
English: 

pp2.4:110.6
Pali: sattahipi dattīhi yāpeti; 
English: 

pp2.4:110.7
Pali: ekāhikampi āhāraṁ āhāreti, dvīhikampi āhāraṁ āhāreti …pe… 
English: 

pp2.4:110.8
Pali: sattāhikampi āhāraṁ āhāreti. 
English: 

pp2.4:110.9
Pali: Iti evarūpaṁ aḍḍhamāsikampi pariyāyabhattabhojanānuyogamanuyutto viharati. 
English: 

pp2.4:110.10
Pali: So sākabhakkho vā hoti sāmākabhakkho vā hoti nīvārabhakkho vā hoti daddulabhakkho vā hoti haṭabhakkho vā hoti kaṇabhakkho vā hoti ācāmabhakkho vā hoti piññākabhakkho vā hoti tiṇabhakkho vā hoti gomayabhakkho vā hoti, vanamūlaphalāhāro yāpeti pavattaphalabhojī. 
English: 

pp2.4:110.11
Pali: So sāṇānipi dhāreti masāṇānipi dhāreti chavadussānipi dhāreti paṁsukūlānipi dhāreti tirīṭānipi dhāreti ajinampi dhāreti ajinakkhipampi dhāreti kusacīrampi dhāreti vākacīrampi dhāreti phalakacīrampi dhāreti kesakambalampi dhāreti vāḷakambalampi dhāreti ulūkapakkhampi dhāreti, kesamassulocakopi hoti kesamassulocanānuyogamanuyutto, ubbhaṭṭhakopi hoti āsanapaṭikkhitto, ukkuṭikopi hoti ukkuṭikappadhānamanuyutto, kaṇṭakāpassayikopi hoti kaṇṭakāpassaye seyyaṁ kappeti, sāyatatiyakampi udakorohanānuyogamanuyutto viharati. 
English: 

pp2.4:110.12
Pali: Iti evarūpaṁ anekavihitaṁ kāyassa ātāpanaparitāpanānuyogamanuyutto viharati.

pp2.4:110.13
Pali: Evaṁ puggalo attantapo hoti attaparitāpanānuyogamanuyutto.

pp2.4:111.1
Pali: Kathañca puggalo parantapo hoti paraparitāpanānuyogamanuyutto? 
English: 

pp2.4:111.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo orabbhiko hoti sūkariko sākuṇiko māgaviko luddo macchaghātako coro coraghātako goghātako bandhanāgāriko, ye vā panaññepi keci kurūrakammantā. 
English: 

pp2.4:111.3
Pali: Evaṁ puggalo parantapo hoti paraparitāpanānuyogamanuyutto. 
English: 

pp2.4:112.1
Pali: Kathañca puggalo attantapo ca hoti attaparitāpanānuyogamanuyutto, parantapo ca paraparitāpanānuyogamanuyutto? 
English: 

pp2.4:112.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo rājā vā hoti khattiyo muddhāvasitto brāhmaṇo vā mahāsālo. 
English: 

pp2.4:112.3
Pali: So puratthimena nagarassa navaṁ sandhāgāraṁ kārāpetvā kesamassuṁ ohāretvā kharājinaṁ nivāsetvā sappitelena kāyaṁ abbhañjitvā migavisāṇena piṭṭhiṁ kaṇḍuvamāno sandhāgāraṁ pavisati saddhiṁ mahesiyā brāhmaṇena ca purohitena. 
English: 

pp2.4:112.4
Pali: So tattha anantarahitāya bhūmiyā haritupalittāya seyyaṁ kappeti. 
English: 

pp2.4:112.5
Pali: Ekissā gāviyā sarūpavacchāya yaṁ ekasmiṁ thane khīraṁ hoti tena rājā yāpeti, yaṁ dutiyasmiṁ thane khīraṁ hoti tena mahesī yāpeti, yaṁ tatiyasmiṁ thane khīraṁ hoti tena brāhmaṇo purohito yāpeti, yaṁ catutthasmiṁ thane khīraṁ hoti tena aggiṁ juhati, avasesena vacchako yāpeti. 
English: 

pp2.4:112.6
Pali: So evamāha—
English: 

pp2.4:112.7
Pali: “ettakā usabhā haññantu yaññatthāya, ettakā vacchatarā haññantu yaññatthāya, ettakā vacchatariyo haññantu yaññatthāya, ettakā ajā haññantu yaññatthāya, ettakā urabbhā haññantu yaññatthāya, ettakā assā haññantu yaññatthāya ettakā rukkhā chijjantu yūpatthāya, ettakā dabbhā lūyantu barihisatthāyā”ti. 
English: 

pp2.4:112.8
Pali: Yepissa te honti dāsāti vā pessāti vā kammakarāti vā, tepi daṇḍatajjitā bhayatajjitā assumukhā rudamānā parikammāni karonti. 
English: 

pp2.4:112.9
Pali: Evaṁ puggalo attantapo ca hoti attaparitāpanānuyogamanuyutto, parantapo ca paraparitāpanānuyogamanuyutto. 
English: 

pp2.4:113.1
Pali: Kathañca puggalo neva attantapo ca hoti na attaparitāpanānuyogamanuyutto, na parantapo na paraparitāpanānuyogamanuyutto? 
English: 

pp2.4:113.2
Pali: So anattantapo aparantapo diṭṭheva dhamme nicchāto nibbuto sītībhūto sukhappaṭisaṁvedī brahmabhūtena attanā viharati. 
English: 

pp2.4:114.1
Pali: Idha tathāgato loke uppajjati arahaṁ sammāsambuddho vijjācaraṇasampanno sugato lokavidū anuttaro purisadammasārathi satthā devamanussānaṁ buddho bhagavā. 
English: 

pp2.4:114.2
Pali: So imaṁ lokaṁ sadevakaṁ samārakaṁ sabrahmakaṁ sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiṁ pajaṁ sadevamanussaṁ sayaṁ abhiññā sacchikatvā pavedeti. 
English: 

pp2.4:114.3
Pali: So dhammaṁ deseti ādikalyāṇaṁ majjhekalyāṇaṁ pariyosānakalyāṇaṁ sātthaṁ sabyañjanaṁ, kevalaparipuṇṇaṁ parisuddhaṁ brahmacariyaṁ pakāseti. 
English: 

pp2.4:114.4
Pali: Taṁ dhammaṁ suṇāti gahapati vā gahapatiputto vā aññatarasmiṁ vā kule paccājāto. 
English: 

pp2.4:114.5
Pali: So taṁ dhammaṁ sutvā tathāgate saddhaṁ paṭilabhati. 
English: 

pp2.4:114.6
Pali: So tena saddhāpaṭilābhena samannāgato iti paṭisañcikkhati—
English: 

pp2.4:114.7
Pali: “sambādho gharāvāso rajāpatho, abbhokāso pabbajjā. 
English: 

pp2.4:114.8
Pali: Nayidaṁ sukaraṁ agāraṁ ajjhāvasatā ekantaparipuṇṇaṁ ekantaparisuddhaṁ saṅkhalikhitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ carituṁ. 
English: 

pp2.4:114.9
Pali: Yannūnāhaṁ kesamassuṁ ohāretvā kāsāyāni vatthāni acchādetvā agārasmā anagāriyaṁ pabbajeyyan”ti. 
English: 

pp2.4:114.10
Pali: So aparena samayena appaṁ vā bhogakkhandhaṁ pahāya mahantaṁ vā bhogakkhandhaṁ pahāya appaṁ vā ñātiparivaṭṭaṁ pahāya mahantaṁ vā ñātiparivaṭṭaṁ pahāya kesamassuṁ ohāretvā kāsāyāni vatthāni acchādetvā agārasmā anagāriyaṁ pabbajati. 
English: 

pp2.4:115.1
Pali: So evaṁ pabbajito samāno bhikkhūnaṁ sikkhāsājīvasamāpanno pāṇātipātaṁ pahāya pāṇātipātā paṭivirato hoti nihitadaṇḍo nihitasattho lajjī dayāpanno sabbapāṇabhūtahitānukampī viharati. 
English: 

pp2.4:116.1
Pali: Adinnādānaṁ pahāya adinnādānā paṭivirato hoti dinnādāyī dinnapāṭikaṅkhī, athenena sucibhūtena attanā viharati. 
English: 

pp2.4:117.1
Pali: Abrahmacariyaṁ pahāya brahmacārī hoti ārācārī paṭivirato methunā gāmadhammā. 
English: 

pp2.4:118.1
Pali: Musāvādaṁ pahāya musāvādā paṭivirato hoti saccavādī saccasandho theto paccayiko avisaṁvādako lokassa. 
English: 

pp2.4:119.1
Pali: Pisuṇaṁ vācaṁ pahāya pisuṇāya vācāya paṭivirato hoti, ito sutvā na amutra akkhātā imesaṁ bhedāya, amutra vā sutvā na imesaṁ akkhātā amūsaṁ bhedāya. 
English: 

pp2.4:119.2
Pali: Iti bhinnānaṁ vā sandhātā sahitānaṁ vā anuppadātā samaggārāmo samaggarato samagganandī samaggakaraṇiṁ vācaṁ bhāsitā hoti. 
English: 

pp2.4:120.1
Pali: Pharusaṁ vācaṁ pahāya pharusāya vācāya paṭivirato hoti. 
English: 

pp2.4:120.2
Pali: Yā sā vācā nelā kaṇṇasukhā pemanīyā hadayaṅgamā porī bahujanakantā bahujanamanāpā tathārūpiṁ vācaṁ bhāsitā hoti. 
English: 

pp2.4:121.1
Pali: Samphappalāpaṁ pahāya samphappalāpā paṭivirato hoti, kālavādī bhūtavādī atthavādī dhammavādī vinayavādī nidhānavatiṁ vācaṁ bhāsitā kālena sāpadesaṁ pariyantavatiṁ atthasaṁhitaṁ. 
English: 

pp2.4:122.1
Pali: So bījagāmabhūtagāmasamārambhā paṭivirato hoti, ekabhattiko hoti rattūparato virato vikālabhojanā, naccagītavāditavisūkadassanā paṭivirato hoti, mālāgandhavilepanadhāraṇamaṇḍanavibhūsanaṭṭhānā paṭivirato hoti, uccāsayanamahāsayanā paṭivirato hoti, jātarūparajatapaṭiggahaṇā paṭivirato hoti. 
English: 

pp2.4:123.1
Pali: Āmakadhaññapaṭiggahaṇā paṭivirato hoti, āmakamaṁsapaṭiggahaṇā paṭivirato hoti, itthikumārikāpaṭiggahaṇā paṭivirato hoti, dāsidāsapaṭiggahaṇā paṭivirato hoti, ajeḷakapaṭiggahaṇā paṭivirato hoti, kukkuṭasūkarapaṭiggahaṇā paṭivirato hoti, hatthigavāssavaḷavapaṭiggahaṇā paṭivirato hoti, khettavatthupaṭiggahaṇā paṭivirato hoti, dūteyyapahiṇagamanānuyogā paṭivirato hoti, kayavikkayā paṭivirato hoti, tulākūṭakaṁsakūṭamānakūṭā paṭivirato hoti, ukkoṭanavañcananikatisāciyogā paṭivirato hoti, chedanavadhabandhanaviparāmosaālopasahasākārā paṭivirato hoti. 
English: 

pp2.4:124.1
Pali: So santuṭṭho hoti kāyaparihārikena cīvarena kucchiparihārikena piṇḍapātena. 
English: 

pp2.4:124.2
Pali: So yena yeneva pakkamati samādāyeva pakkamati, seyyathāpi nāma pakkhī sakuṇo yena yeneva ḍeti sapattabhārova ḍeti. 
English: 

pp2.4:124.3
Pali: Evamevaṁ bhikkhu santuṭṭho hoti kāyaparihārikena cīvarena kucchiparihārikena piṇḍapātena. 
English: 

pp2.4:124.4
Pali: So yena yeneva pakkamati samādāyeva pakkamati. 
English: 

pp2.4:124.5
Pali: So iminā ariyena sīlakkhandhena samannāgato ajjhattaṁ anavajjasukhaṁ paṭisaṁvedeti. 
English: 

pp2.4:125.1
Pali: So cakkhunā rūpaṁ disvā na nimittaggāhī hoti nānubyañjanaggāhī. 
English: 

pp2.4:125.2
Pali: Yatvādhikaraṇamenaṁ cakkhundriyaṁ asaṁvutaṁ viharantaṁ abhijjhādomanassā pāpakā akusalā dhammā anvāssaveyyuṁ, tassa saṁvarāya paṭipajjati, rakkhati cakkhundriyaṁ, cakkhundriye saṁvaraṁ āpajjati; 
English: 

pp2.4:125.3
Pali: sotena saddaṁ sutvā …pe… 
English: 

pp2.4:125.4
Pali: ghānena gandhaṁ ghāyitvā …pe… 
English: 

pp2.4:125.5
Pali: jivhāya rasaṁ sāyitvā …pe… 
English: 

pp2.4:125.6
Pali: kāyena phoṭṭhabbaṁ phusitvā …pe… 
English: 

pp2.4:125.7
Pali: manasā dhammaṁ viññāya na nimittaggāhī hoti nānubyañjanaggāhī. 
English: 

pp2.4:125.8
Pali: Yatvādhikaraṇamenaṁ manindriyaṁ asaṁvutaṁ viharantaṁ abhijjhādomanassā pāpakā akusalā dhammā anvāssaveyyuṁ, tassa saṁvarāya paṭipajjati, rakkhati manindriyaṁ, manindriye saṁvaraṁ āpajjati. 
English: 

pp2.4:125.9
Pali: So iminā ariyena indriyasaṁvarena samannāgato ajjhattaṁ abyāsekasukhaṁ paṭisaṁvedeti. 
English: 

pp2.4:126.1
Pali: So abhikkante paṭikkante sampajānakārī hoti, ālokite vilokite sampajānakārī hoti, samiñjite pasārite sampajānakārī hoti, saṅghāṭipattacīvaradhāraṇe sampajānakārī hoti, asite pīte khāyite sāyite sampajānakārī hoti, uccārapassāvakamme sampajānakārī hoti, gate ṭhite nisinne sutte jāgarite bhāsite tuṇhībhāve sampajānakārī hoti. 
English: 

pp2.4:127.1
Pali: So iminā ca ariyena sīlakkhandhena samannāgato iminā ca ariyena indriyasaṁvarena samannāgato iminā ca ariyena satisampajaññena samannāgato imāya ca ariyāya santuṭṭhiyā samannāgato vivittaṁ senāsanaṁ bhajati araññaṁ rukkhamūlaṁ pabbataṁ kandaraṁ giriguhaṁ susānaṁ vanapatthaṁ abbhokāsaṁ palālapuñjaṁ. 
English: 

pp2.4:127.2
Pali: So pacchābhattaṁ piṇḍapātapaṭikkanto nisīdati pallaṅkaṁ ābhujitvā ujuṁ kāyaṁ paṇidhāya parimukhaṁ satiṁ upaṭṭhapetvā. 
English: 

pp2.4:127.3
Pali: So abhijjhaṁ loke pahāya vigatābhijjhena cetasā viharati, abhijjhāya cittaṁ parisodheti; 
English: 

pp2.4:127.4
Pali: byāpādapadosaṁ pahāya abyāpannacitto viharati sabbapāṇabhūtahitānukampī, byāpādapadosā cittaṁ parisodheti; 
English: 

pp2.4:127.5
Pali: thinamiddhaṁ pahāya vigatathinamiddho viharati ālokasaññī sato sampajāno, thinamiddhā cittaṁ parisodheti; 
English: 

pp2.4:127.6
Pali: uddhaccakukkuccaṁ pahāya anuddhato viharati ajjhattaṁ vūpasantacitto, uddhaccakukkuccā cittaṁ parisodheti; 
English: 

pp2.4:127.7
Pali: vicikicchaṁ pahāya tiṇṇavicikiccho viharati akathaṅkathī kusalesu dhammesu, vicikicchāya cittaṁ parisodheti. 
English: 

pp2.4:128.1
Pali: So ime pañca nīvaraṇe pahāya cetaso upakkilese paññāya dubbalīkaraṇe vivicceva kāmehi vivicca akusalehi dhammehi savitakkaṁ savicāraṁ vivekajaṁ pītisukhaṁ paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati; 
English: 

pp2.4:128.2
Pali: vitakkavicārānaṁ vūpasamā ajjhattaṁ sampasādanaṁ cetaso ekodibhāvaṁ avitakkaṁ avicāraṁ samādhijaṁ pītisukhaṁ dutiyaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati; 
English: 

pp2.4:128.3
Pali: pītiyā ca virāgā upekkhako ca viharati sato ca sampajāno sukhañca kāyena paṭisaṁvedeti, yaṁ taṁ ariyā ācikkhanti—“upekkhako satimā sukhavihārī”ti tatiyaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati; 
English: 

pp2.4:128.4
Pali: sukhassa ca pahānā dukkhassa ca pahānā pubbeva somanassadomanassānaṁ atthaṅgamā adukkhamasukhaṁ upekkhāsatipārisuddhiṁ catutthaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati. 
English: 

pp2.4:129.1
Pali: So evaṁ samāhite citte parisuddhe pariyodāte anaṅgaṇe vigatūpakkilese mudubhūte kammaniye ṭhite āneñjappatte pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇāya cittaṁ abhininnāmeti. 
English: 

pp2.4:129.2
Pali: So anekavihitaṁ pubbenivāsaṁ anussarati, seyyathidaṁ—
English: 

pp2.4:129.3
Pali: ekampi jātiṁ dvepi jātiyo tissopi jātiyo catassopi jātiyo pañcapi jātiyo dasapi jātiyo vīsampi jātiyo tiṁsampi jātiyo cattālīsampi jātiyo paññāsampi jātiyo jātisatampi jātisahassampi jātisatasahassampi anekepi saṁvaṭṭakappe anekepi vivaṭṭakappe anekepi saṁvaṭṭavivaṭṭakappe—
English: 

pp2.4:129.4
Pali: “amutrāsiṁ evaṁnāmo evaṅgotto evaṁvaṇṇo evamāhāro evaṁsukhadukkhapaṭisaṁvedī evamāyupariyanto, so tato cuto amutra udapādiṁ; 
English: 

pp2.4:129.5
Pali: tatrāpāsiṁ evaṁnāmo evaṅgotto evaṁvaṇṇo evamāhāro evaṁsukhadukkhapaṭisaṁvedī evamāyupariyanto, so tato cuto idhūpapanno”ti. 
English: 

pp2.4:129.6
Pali: Iti sākāraṁ sauddesaṁ anekavihitaṁ pubbenivāsaṁ anussarati. 
English: 

pp2.4:130.1
Pali: So evaṁ samāhite citte parisuddhe pariyodāte anaṅgaṇe vigatūpakkilese mudubhūte kammaniye ṭhite āneñjappatte sattānaṁ cutūpapātañāṇāya cittaṁ abhininnāmeti. 
English: 

pp2.4:130.2
Pali: So dibbena cakkhunā visuddhena atikkantamānusakena satte passati cavamāne upapajjamāne hīne paṇīte suvaṇṇe dubbaṇṇe, sugate duggate yathākammūpage satte pajānāti—
English: 

pp2.4:130.3
Pali: “ime vata bhonto sattā kāyaduccaritena samannāgatā, vacīduccaritena samannāgatā, manoduccaritena samannāgatā, ariyānaṁ upavādakā, micchādiṭṭhikā micchādiṭṭhikammasamādānā. 
English: 

pp2.4:130.4
Pali: Te kāyassa bhedā paraṁ maraṇā apāyaṁ duggatiṁ vinipātaṁ nirayaṁ upapannā. 
English: 

pp2.4:130.5
Pali: Ime vā pana bhonto sattā kāyasucaritena samannāgatā vacīsucaritena samannāgatā manosucaritena samannāgatā ariyānaṁ anupavādakā sammādiṭṭhikā sammādiṭṭhikammasamādānā. 
English: 

pp2.4:130.6
Pali: Te kāyassa bhedā paraṁ maraṇā sugatiṁ saggaṁ lokaṁ upapannā”ti. 
English: 

pp2.4:130.7
Pali: So iti dibbena cakkhunā visuddhena atikkantamānusakena satte passati cavamāne upapajjamāne hīne paṇīte suvaṇṇe dubbaṇṇe, sugate duggate yathākammūpage satte pajānāti. 
English: 

pp2.4:131.1
Pali: So evaṁ samāhite citte parisuddhe pariyodāte anaṅgaṇe vigatūpakkilese mudubhūte kammaniye ṭhite āneñjappatte āsavānaṁ khayañāṇāya cittaṁ abhininnāmeti. 
English: 

pp2.4:131.2
Pali: So “idaṁ dukkhan”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, “ayaṁ dukkhasamudayo”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, “ayaṁ dukkhanirodho”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, “ayaṁ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, 
English: 

pp2.4:131.3
Pali: “ime āsavā”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, “ayaṁ āsavasamudayo”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, “ayaṁ āsavanirodho”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, “ayaṁ āsavanirodhagāminī paṭipadā”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti. 
English: 

pp2.4:131.4
Pali: Tassa evaṁ jānato evaṁ passato kāmāsavāpi cittaṁ vimuccati, bhavāsavāpi cittaṁ vimuccati, avijjāsavāpi cittaṁ vimuccati. 
English: 

pp2.4:131.5
Pali: Vimuttasmiṁ vimuttamiti ñāṇaṁ hoti. 
English: 

pp2.4:131.6
Pali: “Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā”ti pajānāti. 
English: 

pp2.4:131.7
Pali: Evaṁ puggalo neva attantapo ca hoti na attaparitāpanānuyogamanuyutto, na parantapo na paraparitāpanānuyogamanuyutto. 
English: 

pp2.4:131.8
Pali: So anattantapo aparantapo diṭṭheva dhamme nicchāto nibbuto sītībhūto sukhappaṭisaṁvedī brahmabhūtena attanā viharati. 
English: 

pp2.4:132.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo sarāgo?

pp2.4:132.2

pp2.4:139.3

pp2.4:141.3
Pali: So sahāpi dukkhena sahāpi domanassena assumukhenapi rudamāno paripuṇṇaṁ parisuddhaṁ brahmacariyaṁ carati.

pp2.5
Root: root/pli/ms/abhidhamma/pp/pp2/pp2.5_root-pli-ms.json

pp2.5:0.1
Pali: Puggalapaññatti 
English: 

pp2.5:0.2
Pali: Niddesa 
English: 

pp2.5:0.3
Pali: 5. Pañcakapuggalapaññatti 
English: 

pp2.5:1.1
Pali: Tatra yvāyaṁ puggalo ārabhati ca vippaṭisārī ca hoti, tañca cetovimuttiṁ paññāvimuttiṁ yathābhūtaṁ nappajānāti, yatthassa te uppannā pāpakā akusalā dhammā aparisesā nirujjhanti, so evamassa vacanīyo—
English: 

pp2.5:1.2
Pali: “āyasmato kho ārambhajā āsavā saṁvijjanti, vippaṭisārajā āsavā pavaḍḍhanti. 
English: 

pp2.5:1.3
Pali: Sādhu vatāyasmā ārambhaje āsave pahāya vippaṭisāraje āsave paṭivinodetvā cittaṁ paññañca bhāvetu. 
English: 

pp2.5:1.4
Pali: Evamāyasmā amunā pañcamena puggalena samasamo bhavissatī”ti. 
English: 

pp2.5:2.1
Pali: Tatra yvāyaṁ puggalo ārabhati na vippaṭisārī hoti, tañca cetovimuttiṁ paññāvimuttiṁ yathābhūtaṁ nappajānāti, yatthassa te uppannā pāpakā akusalā dhammā aparisesā nirujjhanti, so evamassa vacanīyo—
English: 

pp2.5:2.2
Pali: “āyasmato kho ārambhajā āsavā saṁvijjanti, vippaṭisārajā āsavā nappavaḍḍhanti. 
English: 

pp2.5:2.3
Pali: Sādhu vatāyasmā ārambhaje āsave pahāya cittaṁ paññañca bhāvetu. 
English: 

pp2.5:2.4
Pali: Evamāyasmā amunā pañcamena puggalena samasamo bhavissatī”ti. 
English: 

pp2.5:3.1
Pali: Tatra yvāyaṁ puggalo na ārabhati vippaṭisārī hoti, tañca cetovimuttiṁ paññāvimuttiṁ yathābhūtaṁ nappajānāti, yatthassa te uppannā pāpakā akusalā dhammā aparisesā nirujjhanti, so evamassa vacanīyo—
English: 

pp2.5:3.2
Pali: “āyasmato kho ārambhajā āsavā na saṁvijjanti, vippaṭisārajā āsavā pavaḍḍhanti. 
English: 

pp2.5:3.3
Pali: Sādhu vatāyasmā vippaṭisāraje āsave paṭivinodetvā cittaṁ paññañca bhāvetu. 
English: 

pp2.5:3.4
Pali: Evamāyasmā amunā pañcamena puggalena samasamo bhavissatī”ti. 
English: 

pp2.5:4.1
Pali: Tatra yvāyaṁ puggalo na ārabhati na vippaṭisārī hoti, tañca cetovimuttiṁ paññāvimuttiṁ yathābhūtaṁ nappajānāti, yatthassa te pāpakā akusalā dhammā aparisesā nirujjhanti, so evamassa vacanīyo—
English: 

pp2.5:4.2
Pali: “āyasmato kho ārambhajā āsavā na saṁvijjanti, vippaṭisārajā āsavā nappavaḍḍhanti. 
English: 

pp2.5:4.3
Pali: Sādhu vatāyasmā cittaṁ paññañca bhāvetu. 
English: 

pp2.5:4.4
Pali: Evamāyasmā amunā pañcamena puggalena samasamo bhavissatī”ti. 
English: 

pp2.5:5.1
Pali: Ime cattāro puggalā amunā pañcamena puggalena evaṁ ovadiyamānā evaṁ anusāsiyamānā anupubbena āsavānaṁ khayaṁ pāpuṇanti. 
English: 

pp2.5:6.1
Pali: Kathañca puggalo datvā avajānāti? 
English: 

pp2.5:6.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo yassa puggalassa deti cīvarapiṇḍapātasenāsanagilānapaccayabhesajjaparikkhāraṁ, tassa evaṁ hoti—
English: 

pp2.5:6.3
Pali: “ahaṁ dammi, ayaṁ paṭiggaṇhātī”ti, tamenaṁ datvā avajānāti. 
English: 

pp2.5:6.4
Pali: Evaṁ puggalo datvā avajānāti. 
English: 

pp2.5:7.1
Pali: Kathañca puggalo saṁvāsena avajānāti? 
English: 

pp2.5:7.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo yena puggalena saddhiṁ saṁvasati dve vā tīṇi vā vassāni, tamenaṁ saṁvāsena avajānāti. 
English: 

pp2.5:7.3
Pali: Evaṁ puggalo saṁvāsena avajānāti. 
English: 

pp2.5:8.1
Pali: Kathañca puggalo ādheyyamukho hoti? 
English: 

pp2.5:8.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo parassa vaṇṇe vā avaṇṇe vā bhāsiyamāne khippaññeva adhimuccitā hoti. 
English: 

pp2.5:8.3
Pali: Evaṁ puggalo ādheyyamukho hoti. 
English: 

pp2.5:9.1
Pali: Kathañca puggalo lolo hoti? 
English: 

pp2.5:9.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo ittarasaddho hoti ittarabhattī ittarapemo ittarappasādo. 
English: 

pp2.5:9.3
Pali: Evaṁ puggalo lolo hoti. 
English: 

pp2.5:10.1
Pali: Kathañca puggalo mando momūho hoti? 
English: 

pp2.5:10.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo kusalākusale dhamme na jānāti, sāvajjānavajje dhamme na jānāti, hīnappaṇīte dhamme na jānāti, kaṇhasukkasappaṭibhāge dhamme na jānāti. 
English: 

pp2.5:10.3
Pali: Evaṁ puggalo mando momūho hoti. 
English: 

pp2.5:11.1
Pali: Tattha katame pañca yodhājīvūpamā puggalā? 
English: 

pp2.5:11.2
Pali: Pañca yodhājīvā—
English: 

pp2.5:11.3
Pali: idhekacco yodhājīvo rajaggaññeva disvā saṁsīdati visīdati na santhambhati na sakkoti saṅgāmaṁ otarituṁ. 
English: 

pp2.5:11.4
Pali: Evarūpopi idhekacco yodhājīvo hoti. 
English: 

pp2.5:11.5
Pali: Ayaṁ paṭhamo yodhājīvo santo saṁvijjamāno lokasmiṁ. 
English: 

pp2.5:12.1
Pali: Puna caparaṁ idhekacco yodhājīvo sahati rajaggaṁ, api ca kho dhajaggaññeva disvā saṁsīdati visīdati na santhambhati na sakkoti saṅgāmaṁ otarituṁ. 
English: 

pp2.5:12.2
Pali: Evarūpopi idhekacco yodhājīvo hoti. 
English: 

pp2.5:12.3
Pali: Ayaṁ dutiyo yodhājīvo santo saṁvijjamāno lokasmiṁ. 
English: 

pp2.5:13.1
Pali: Puna caparaṁ idhekacco yodhājīvo sahati rajaggaṁ sahati dhajaggaṁ, api ca kho ussāraṇaññeva sutvā saṁsīdati visīdati na santhambhati na sakkoti saṅgāmaṁ otarituṁ. 
English: 

pp2.5:13.2
Pali: Evarūpopi idhekacco yodhājīvo hoti. 
English: 

pp2.5:13.3
Pali: Ayaṁ tatiyo yodhājīvo santo saṁvijjamāno lokasmiṁ. 
English: 

pp2.5:14.1
Pali: Puna caparaṁ idhekacco yodhājīvo sahati rajaggaṁ sahati dhajaggaṁ sahati ussāraṇaṁ, api ca kho sampahāre haññati byāpajjati. 
English: 

pp2.5:14.2
Pali: Evarūpopi idhekacco yodhājīvo hoti. 
English: 

pp2.5:14.3
Pali: Ayaṁ catuttho yodhājīvo santo saṁvijjamāno lokasmiṁ. 
English: 

pp2.5:15.1
Pali: Puna caparaṁ idhekacco yodhājīvo sahati rajaggaṁ sahati dhajaggaṁ sahati ussāraṇaṁ sahati sampahāraṁ. 
English: 

pp2.5:15.2
Pali: So taṁ saṅgāmaṁ abhivijinitvā vijitasaṅgāmo tameva saṅgāmasīsaṁ ajjhāvasati.

pp2.5:15.3
Pali: Evarūpopi idhekacco yodhājīvo hoti.

pp2.5:15.4

pp2.5:15.5
Pali: Ime pañca yodhājīvā santo saṁvijjamānā lokasmiṁ. 
English: 

pp2.5:16.1
Pali: Evamevaṁ pañcime yodhājīvūpamā puggalā santo saṁvijjamānā bhikkhūsu. 
English: 

pp2.5:16.2
Pali: Katame pañca? 
English: 

pp2.5:17.1
Pali: Idhekacco bhikkhu rajaggaññeva disvā saṁsīdati visīdati na santhambhati na sakkoti brahmacariyaṁ sandhāretuṁ, sikkhādubbalyaṁ āvikatvā sikkhaṁ paccakkhāya hīnāyāvattati. 
English: 

pp2.5:17.2
Pali: Kimassa rajaggasmiṁ? 
English: 

pp2.5:17.3
Pali: Idha bhikkhu suṇāti—
English: 

pp2.5:17.4
Pali: “asukasmiṁ nāma gāme vā nigame vā itthī vā kumārī vā abhirūpā dassanīyā pāsādikā paramāya vaṇṇapokkharatāya samannāgatā”ti. 
English: 

pp2.5:17.5
Pali: So taṁ sutvā saṁsīdati visīdati na santhambhati na sakkoti brahmacariyaṁ sandhāretuṁ, sikkhādubbalyaṁ āvikatvā sikkhaṁ paccakkhāya hīnāyāvattati. 
English: 

pp2.5:17.6
Pali: Idamassa rajaggasmiṁ. 
English: 

pp2.5:18.1
Pali: Seyyathāpi so yodhājīvo rajaggaññeva disvā saṁsīdati visīdati na santhambhati na sakkoti saṅgāmaṁ otarituṁ, tathūpamo ayaṁ puggalo. 
English: 

pp2.5:18.2
Pali: Evarūpopi idhekacco puggalo hoti.

pp2.5:18.3
Pali: Ayaṁ paṭhamo yodhājīvūpamo puggalo santo saṁvijjamāno bhikkhūsu. 
English: 

pp2.5:19.1
Pali: Puna caparaṁ idhekacco bhikkhu sahati rajaggaṁ, api ca kho dhajaggaññeva disvā saṁsīdati visīdati na santhambhati na sakkoti brahmacariyaṁ sandhāretuṁ, sikkhādubbalyaṁ āvikatvā sikkhaṁ paccakkhāya hīnāyāvattati. 
English: 

pp2.5:19.2
Pali: Kimassa dhajaggasmiṁ? 
English: 

pp2.5:19.3
Pali: Idha bhikkhu na heva kho suṇāti—
English: 

pp2.5:19.4
Pali: “asukasmiṁ nāma gāme vā nigame vā itthī vā kumārī vā abhirūpā dassanīyā pāsādikā paramāya vaṇṇapokkharatāya samannāgatā”ti, api ca kho sāmaṁ passati itthiṁ vā kumāriṁ vā abhirūpaṁ dassanīyaṁ pāsādikaṁ paramāya vaṇṇapokkharatāya samannāgataṁ. 
English: 

pp2.5:19.5
Pali: So taṁ disvā saṁsīdati visīdati na santhambhati na sakkoti brahmacariyaṁ sandhāretuṁ, sikkhādubbalyaṁ āvikatvā sikkhaṁ paccakkhāya hīnāyāvattati. 
English: 

pp2.5:19.6
Pali: Idamassa dhajaggasmiṁ. 
English:

Pali: Seyyathāpi so yodhājīvo sahati rajaggaṁ, api ca kho dhajaggaññeva disvā saṁsīdati visīdati na santhambhati na sakkoti saṅgāmaṁ otarituṁ, tathūpamo ayaṁ puggalo.

pp2.5:21.3

English: 

pp2.5:21.4
Pali: So mātugāmena ūhasiyamāno ullapiyamāno ujjagghiyamāno uppaṇḍiyamāno saṁsīdati visīdati na santhambhati na sakkoti brahmacariyaṁ sandhāretuṁ, sikkhādubbalyaṁ āvikatvā sikkhaṁ paccakkhāya hīnāyāvattati. 
English: 

pp2.5:21.5
Pali: Idamassa ussāraṇāya.

pp2.5:22.1

English: 

pp2.5:23.2
Pali: Kimassa sampahārasmiṁ? 
English: 

pp2.5:23.3
Pali: Idha bhikkhuṁ araññagataṁ vā rukkhamūlagataṁ vā suññāgāragataṁ vā mātugāmo upasaṅkamitvā abhinisīdati abhinipajjati ajjhottharati. 
English: 

pp2.5:23.4
Pali: So mātugāmena abhinisīdiyamāno abhinipajjiyamāno ajjhotthariyamāno sikkhaṁ appaccakkhāya dubbalyaṁ anāvikatvā methunaṁ dhammaṁ paṭisevati. 
English: 

pp2.5:23.5
Pali: Idamassa sampahārasmiṁ.

Pali: Seyyathāpi so yodhājīvo sahati rajaggaṁ sahati dhajaggaṁ sahati ussāraṇaṁ, api ca kho sampahāre haññati byāpajjati, tathūpamo ayaṁ puggalo.

pp2.5:25.1
Pali: Puna caparaṁ idhekacco bhikkhu sahati rajaggaṁ sahati dhajaggaṁ sahati ussāraṇaṁ sahati sampahāraṁ. 
English: 

pp2.5:25.2
Pali: So taṁ saṅgāmaṁ abhivijinitvā vijitasaṅgāmo tameva saṅgāmasīsaṁ ajjhāvasati. 
English: 

pp2.5:25.3
Pali: Kimassa saṅgāmavijayasmiṁ? 
English: 

pp2.5:25.4
Pali: Idha bhikkhuṁ araññagataṁ vā rukkhamūlagataṁ vā suññāgāragataṁ vā mātugāmo upasaṅkamitvā abhinisīdati abhinipajjati ajjhottharati. 
English: 

pp2.5:25.5
Pali: So mātugāmena abhinisīdiyamāno abhinipajjiyamāno ajjhotthariyamāno viniveṭhetvā vinimocetvā yena kāmaṁ pakkamati. 
English: 

pp2.5:26.1
Pali: So vivittaṁ senāsanaṁ bhajati araññaṁ rukkhamūlaṁ pabbataṁ kandaraṁ giriguhaṁ susānaṁ vanapatthaṁ abbhokāsaṁ palālapuñjaṁ. 
English: 

pp2.5:26.2
Pali: So araññagato vā rukkhamūlagato vā suññāgāragato vā nisīdati pallaṅkaṁ ābhujitvā ujuṁ kāyaṁ paṇidhāya parimukhaṁ satiṁ upaṭṭhapetvā. 
English: 

pp2.5:26.3
Pali: So abhijjhaṁ loke pahāya vigatābhijjhena cetasā viharati, abhijjhāya cittaṁ parisodheti; 
English: 

pp2.5:26.4
Pali: byāpādapadosaṁ pahāya abyāpannacitto viharati, sabbapāṇabhūtahitānukampī byāpādapadosā cittaṁ parisodheti; 
English: 

pp2.5:26.5
Pali: thinamiddhaṁ pahāya vigatathinamiddho viharati ālokasaññī sato sampajāno, thinamiddhā cittaṁ parisodheti; 
English: 

pp2.5:26.6
Pali: uddhaccakukkuccaṁ pahāya anuddhato viharati ajjhattaṁ vūpasantacitto, uddhaccakukkuccā cittaṁ parisodheti; 
English: 

pp2.5:26.7
Pali: vicikicchaṁ pahāya tiṇṇavicikiccho viharati akathaṅkathī kusalesu dhammesu, vicikicchāya cittaṁ parisodheti. 
English: 

pp2.5:27.1
Pali: So ime pañca nīvaraṇe pahāya cetaso upakkilese paññāya dubbalīkaraṇe vivicceva kāmehi vivicca akusalehi dhammehi savitakkaṁ savicāraṁ vivekajaṁ pītisukhaṁ paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati; 
English: 

pp2.5:27.2
Pali: vitakkavicārānaṁ vūpasamā dutiyaṁ jhānaṁ …pe… 
English: 

pp2.5:27.3
Pali: tatiyaṁ jhānaṁ …pe…

pp2.5:27.4
Pali: catutthaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati. 
English: 

pp2.5:28.1
Pali: So evaṁ samāhite citte parisuddhe pariyodāte anaṅgaṇe vigatūpakkilese mudubhūte kammaniye ṭhite āneñjappatte āsavānaṁ khayañāṇāya cittaṁ abhininnāmeti. 
English: 

pp2.5:28.2
Pali: So “idaṁ dukkhan”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, “ayaṁ dukkhasamudayo”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, “ayaṁ dukkhanirodho”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, “ayaṁ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadā”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, 
English: 

pp2.5:28.3
Pali: “ime āsavā”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, “ayaṁ āsavasamudayo”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, “ayaṁ āsavanirodho”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, “ayaṁ āsavanirodhagāminī paṭipadā”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti. 
English: 

pp2.5:29.1
Pali: Tassa evaṁ jānato evaṁ passato kāmāsavāpi cittaṁ vimuccati, bhavāsavāpi cittaṁ vimuccati, avijjāsavāpi cittaṁ vimuccati. 
English: 

pp2.5:29.2
Pali: Vimuttasmiṁ vimuttamiti ñāṇaṁ hoti. 
English: 

pp2.5:29.3
Pali: “Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā”ti pajānāti. 
English: 

pp2.5:29.4
Pali: Idamassa saṅgāmavijayasmiṁ. 
English: 

pp2.5:29.5
Pali: Seyyathāpi so yodhājīvo sahati rajaggaṁ sahati dhajaggaṁ sahati ussāraṇaṁ sahati sampahāraṁ, so taṁ saṅgāmaṁ abhivijinitvā vijitasaṅgāmo tameva saṅgāmasīsaṁ ajjhāvasati, tathūpamo ayaṁ puggalo.

pp2.5:30.1
Pali: Ime pañca yodhājīvūpamā puggalā santo saṁvijjamānā bhikkhūsu. 
English: 

pp2.5:31.1
Pali: Tattha katame pañca piṇḍapātikā? 
English: 

pp2.5:31.2
Pali: Mandattā momūhattā piṇḍapātiko hoti, pāpiccho icchāpakato piṇḍapātiko hoti, ummādā cittavikkhepā piṇḍapātiko hoti, “vaṇṇitaṁ buddhehi buddhasāvakehī”ti piṇḍapātiko hoti, api ca appicchataṁyeva nissāya santuṭṭhiṁyeva nissāya sallekhaṁyeva nissāya idamatthitaṁyeva nissāya piṇḍapātiko hoti. 
English: 

pp2.5:31.3
Pali: Tatra yvāyaṁ piṇḍapātiko appicchataṁyeva nissāya santuṭṭhiṁyeva nissāya sallekhaṁyeva nissāya idamatthitaṁyeva nissāya piṇḍapātiko, ayaṁ imesaṁ pañcannaṁ piṇḍapātikānaṁ aggo ca seṭṭho ca pāmokkho ca uttamo ca pavaro ca. 
English: 

pp2.5:32.1
Pali: Seyyathāpi nāma gavā khīraṁ, khīramhā dadhi, dadhimhā navanītaṁ, navanītamhā sappi, sappimhā sappimaṇḍo, sappimaṇḍaṁ tattha aggamakkhāyati; 
English: 

pp2.5:32.2
Pali: evamevaṁ yvāyaṁ piṇḍapātiko appicchataṁyeva nissāya santuṭṭhiṁyeva nissāya sallekhaṁyeva nissāya idamatthitaṁyeva nissāya piṇḍapātiko hoti, ayaṁ imesaṁ pañcannaṁ piṇḍapātikānaṁ aggo ca seṭṭho ca pāmokkho ca uttamo ca pavaro ca. 
English: 

pp2.5:32.3
Pali: Ime pañca piṇḍapātikā. 
English: 

pp2.5:33.1
Pali: Tattha katame pañca khalupacchābhattikā …pe… 
English: 

pp2.5:33.2
Pali: pañca ekāsanikā …pe…

pp2.5:34.1
Pali: Tattha katame pañca sosānikā? 
English: 

pp2.5:34.2
Pali: Mandattā momūhattā sosāniko hoti, pāpiccho icchāpakato sosāniko hoti, ummādā cittavikkhepā sosāniko hoti, “vaṇṇitaṁ buddhehi buddhasāvakehī”ti sosāniko hoti, api ca appicchataṁyeva nissāya santuṭṭhiṁyeva nissāya sallekhaṁyeva nissāya idamatthitaṁyeva nissāya sosāniko hoti. 
English: 

pp2.5:34.3
Pali: Tatra yvāyaṁ sosāniko appicchataṁyeva nissāya santuṭṭhiṁyeva nissāya sallekhaṁyeva nissāya idamatthitaṁyeva nissāya sosāniko, ayaṁ imesaṁ pañcannaṁ sosānikānaṁ aggo ca seṭṭho ca pāmokkho ca uttamo ca pavaro ca. 
English: 

pp2.5:35.1
Pali: Seyyathāpi nāma gavā khīraṁ, khīramhā dadhi, dadhimhā navanītaṁ, navanītamhā sappi, sappimhā sappimaṇḍo, sappimaṇḍaṁ tattha aggamakkhāyati; 
English: 

pp2.5:35.2
Pali: evamevaṁ yvāyaṁ sosāniko appicchataṁyeva nissāya santuṭṭhiṁyeva nissāya sallekhaṁyeva nissāya idamatthitaṁyeva nissāya sosāniko hoti, ayaṁ imesaṁ pañcannaṁ sosānikānaṁ aggo ca seṭṭho ca pāmokkho ca uttamo ca pavaro ca. 
English: 

pp2.5:35.3
Pali: Ime pañca sosānikā. 
English: 

pp2.5:36.1
Pali: Pañcakaniddeso.

pp2.6:0.1
Pali: Puggalapaññatti 
English: 

pp2.6:0.2
Pali: Niddesa 
English: 

pp2.6:0.3
Pali: 6. Chakkapuggalapaññatti 
English: 

pp2.6:1.1
Pali: Tatra yvāyaṁ puggalo pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu sāmaṁ saccāni abhisambujjhati, tattha ca sabbaññutaṁ pāpuṇāti balesu ca vasībhāvaṁ, sammāsambuddho tena daṭṭhabbo. 
English: 

pp2.6:2.1
Pali: Tatra yvāyaṁ puggalo pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu sāmaṁ saccāni abhisambujjhati, na ca tattha sabbaññutaṁ pāpuṇāti na ca balesu vasībhāvaṁ, paccekasambuddho tena daṭṭhabbo. 
English: 

pp2.6:3.1
Pali: Tatra yvāyaṁ puggalo pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu sāmaṁ saccāni anabhisambujjhati, diṭṭheva dhamme dukkhassantakaro hoti, sāvakapāramiñca pāpuṇāti, sāriputtamoggallānā tena daṭṭhabbā. 
English: 

pp2.6:4.1
Pali: Tatra yvāyaṁ puggalo pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu sāmaṁ saccāni anabhisambujjhati, diṭṭheva dhamme dukkhassantakaro hoti, na ca sāvakapāramiṁ pāpuṇāti, avasesā arahantā tena daṭṭhabbā. 
English: 

pp2.6:5.1
Pali: Tatra yvāyaṁ puggalo pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu sāmaṁ saccāni anabhisambujjhati, na ca diṭṭheva dhamme dukkhassantakaro hoti, anāgāmī hoti anāgantā itthattaṁ, anāgāmī tena daṭṭhabbo. 
English: 

pp2.6:6.1
Pali: Tatra yvāyaṁ puggalo pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu sāmaṁ saccāni anabhisambujjhati, na ca diṭṭheva dhamme dukkhassantakaro hoti, āgantā itthattaṁ, sotāpannasakadāgāmino tena daṭṭhabbā. 
English: 

pp2.6:7.1
Pali: Chakkaniddeso. 
English:

pp2.7:0.1
Pali: Puggalapaññatti 
English: 

pp2.7:0.2
Pali: Niddesa 
English: 

pp2.7:0.3
Pali: 7. Sattakapuggalapaññatti 
English: 

pp2.7:1.1
Pali: Kathañca puggalo sakiṁ nimuggo nimuggova hoti? 
English: 

pp2.7:1.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo samannāgato hoti ekantakāḷakehi akusalehi dhammehi. 
English: 

pp2.7:1.3
Pali: Evaṁ puggalo sakiṁ nimuggo nimuggova hoti. 
English: 

pp2.7:2.1
Pali: Kathañca puggalo ummujjitvā nimujjati? 
English: 

pp2.7:2.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo ummujjati “sāhu saddhā kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu hirī kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu ottappaṁ kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu vīriyaṁ kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu paññā kusalesu dhammesū”ti. 
English: 

pp2.7:2.3
Pali: Tassa sā saddhā neva tiṭṭhati no vaḍḍhati hāyatiyeva, tassa sā hirī neva tiṭṭhati no vaḍḍhati hāyatiyeva, tassa taṁ ottappaṁ neva tiṭṭhati no vaḍḍhati hāyatiyeva, tassa taṁ vīriyaṁ neva tiṭṭhati no vaḍḍhati hāyatiyeva, tassa sā paññā neva tiṭṭhati no vaḍḍhati hāyatiyeva. 
English: 

pp2.7:2.4
Pali: Evaṁ puggalo ummujjitvā nimujjati. 
English: 

pp2.7:3.1
Pali: Kathañca puggalo ummujjitvā ṭhito hoti? 
English: 

pp2.7:3.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo ummujjati “sāhu saddhā kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu hirī kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu ottappaṁ kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu vīriyaṁ kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu paññā kusalesu dhammesū”ti. 
English: 

pp2.7:3.3
Pali: Tassa sā saddhā neva hāyati no vaḍḍhati ṭhitā hoti, tassa sā hirī neva hāyati no vaḍḍhati ṭhitā hoti, tassa taṁ ottappaṁ neva hāyati no vaḍḍhati ṭhitaṁ hoti, tassa taṁ vīriyaṁ neva hāyati no vaḍḍhati ṭhitaṁ hoti, tassa sā paññā neva hāyati no vaḍḍhati ṭhitā hoti. 
English: 

pp2.7:3.4
Pali: Evaṁ puggalo ummujjitvā ṭhito hoti. 
English: 

pp2.7:4.1
Pali: Kathañca puggalo ummujjitvā vipassati viloketi? 
English: 

pp2.7:4.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo ummujjati “sāhu saddhā kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu hirī kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu ottappaṁ kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu vīriyaṁ kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu paññā kusalesu dhammesū”ti. 
English: 

pp2.7:4.3
Pali: So tiṇṇaṁ saṁyojanānaṁ parikkhayā sotāpanno hoti avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano. 
English: 

pp2.7:4.4
Pali: Evaṁ puggalo ummujjitvā vipassati viloketi. 
English: 

pp2.7:5.1
Pali: Kathañca puggalo ummujjitvā patarati? 
English: 

pp2.7:5.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo ummujjati “sāhu saddhā kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu hirī kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu ottappaṁ kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu vīriyaṁ kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu paññā kusalesu dhammesū”ti. 
English: 

pp2.7:5.3
Pali: So tiṇṇaṁ saṁyojanānaṁ parikkhayā rāgadosamohānaṁ tanuttā sakadāgāmī hoti sakideva imaṁ lokaṁ āgantvā dukkhassantakaro hoti. 
English: 

pp2.7:5.4
Pali: Evaṁ puggalo ummujjitvā patarati. 
English: 

pp2.7:6.1
Pali: Kathañca puggalo ummujjitvā patigādhappatto hoti? 
English: 

pp2.7:6.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo ummujjati “sāhu saddhā kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu hirī kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu ottappaṁ kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu vīriyaṁ kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu paññā kusalesu dhammesū”ti. 
English: 

pp2.7:6.3
Pali: So pañcannaṁ orambhāgiyānaṁ saṁyojanānaṁ parikkhayā opapātiko hoti tattha parinibbāyī anāvattidhammo tasmā lokā. 
English: 

pp2.7:6.4
Pali: Evaṁ puggalo ummujjitvā paṭigādhappatto hoti. 
English: 

pp2.7:7.1
Pali: Kathañca puggalo ummujjitvā tiṇṇo hoti pāraṅgato thale tiṭṭhati brāhmaṇo? 
English: 

pp2.7:7.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo ummujjati “sāhu saddhā kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu hirī kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu ottappaṁ kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu vīriyaṁ kusalesu dhammesu, sādhu paññā kusalesu dhammesū”ti. 
English: 

pp2.7:7.3
Pali: So āsavānaṁ khayā anāsavaṁ cetovimuttiṁ paññāvimuttiṁ diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṁ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharati. 
English: 

pp2.7:7.4
Pali: Evaṁ puggalo ummujjitvā tiṇṇo hoti pāraṅgato thale tiṭṭhati brāhmaṇo. 
English: 

pp2.7:8.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo ubhatobhāgavimutto? 
English: 

pp2.7:8.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo aṭṭha vimokkhe kāyena phusitvā viharati paññāya cassa disvā āsavā parikkhīṇā honti. 
English: 

pp2.7:8.3
Pali: Ayaṁ vuccati puggalo ubhatobhāgavimutto. 
English: 

pp2.7:9.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo paññāvimutto …pe…. 
English: 

pp2.7:10.1
Pali: Kāyasakkhī …. 
English: 

pp2.7:11.1
Pali: Diṭṭhippatto …. 
English: 

pp2.7:12.1
Pali: Saddhāvimutto …. 
English: 

pp2.7:13.1
Pali: Dhammānusārī …. 
English: 

pp2.7:14.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo saddhānusārī? 
English: 

pp2.7:14.2
Pali: Yassa puggalassa sotāpattiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipannassa saddhindriyaṁ adhimattaṁ hoti, saddhāvāhiṁ saddhāpubbaṅgamaṁ ariyamaggaṁ bhāveti. 
English: 

pp2.7:14.3
Pali: Ayaṁ vuccati puggalo saddhānusārī. 
English: 

pp2.7:14.4
Pali: Sotāpattiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipanno puggalo saddhānusārī, phale ṭhito saddhāvimuttoti. 
English: 

pp2.7:15.1
Pali: Sattakaniddeso.

English: 

pp2.9:2.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo paccekasambuddho? 
English: 

pp2.9:2.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu sāmaṁ saccāni abhisambujjhati, na ca tattha sabbaññutaṁ pāpuṇāti na ca balesu vasībhāvaṁ. 
English:

English: 

pp2.9:4.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo na heva kho aṭṭha vimokkhe kāyena phusitvā viharati paññāya cassa disvā āsavā parikkhīṇā honti. 
English: 

pp2.9:4.3

pp2.9:5.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo aṭṭha vimokkhe kāyena phusitvā viharati paññāya cassa disvā ekacce āsavā parikkhīṇā honti. 
English: 

pp2.9:5.3
Pali: Ayaṁ vuccati puggalo kāyasakkhī. 
English: 

pp2.9:6.1
Pali: Katamo ca puggalo diṭṭhippatto? 
English: 

pp2.9:6.2
Pali: Idhekacco puggalo “idaṁ dukkhan”ti yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti …pe… 
English:

English:

pp2.9:7.4

Pali: Ayaṁ vuccati puggalo dhammānusārī. 
English:

pp2.10:1.1

English:

pp2.10:5.1
Pali: Puggalapaññattipakaraṇaṁ niṭṭhitaṁ. 
English:
